if (!q) return; input.value = ''; const match = FAQ.find(f => f.q.toLowerCase() === q.toLowerCase()); if (match) { addMsg(q, 'user'); addMsg(match.r[normeVersion()] || match.r.v2002, 'bot'); return; } const f = getFilters(); if (!f.bat || !f.date) { addMsg('Conseil : Renseignez le type de batiment et la date des travaux ci-dessus pour une reponse plus precise.', 'bot'); } addMsg(q, 'user'); callClaude(q); }, goAdmin() { this.close(); APP.switchTab('admin'); }, showFab() { document.getElementById('claude-fab').style.display = 'flex'; } }; })(); // ── Recherche globale ───────────────────────────────── const SEARCH = (() => { function _getAllDocs() { const results = []; for (const t of THEMES) { if (!t.id || t.id === 'accueil' || t.id === 'admin') continue; const themeLabel = (t.ref ? t.ref + ' ' : '') + (t.titre || t.label); const lists = [ { items: t.procedures || [] }, { items: t.instructions || [] }, { items: t.enreg_vierges || [] } ]; for (const list of lists) { for (const d of list.items) { results.push({ code: d.code || '', titre: d.titre || '', themeId: t.id, themeLabel: themeLabel }); } } for (const s of (t.sections || [])) { for (const d of (s.docs || [])) { results.push({ code: d.code || '', titre: d.titre || '', themeId: t.id, themeLabel: themeLabel }); } } if (t.render === 'personnel' && t.agents) { for (const a of t.agents) { for (const d of (a.docs || [])) { results.push({ code: '', titre: d.titre || '', themeId: t.id, themeLabel: themeLabel }); } } } if (t.calculs) { for (const c of t.calculs) { results.push({ code: '', titre: c.titre || '', themeId: t.id, themeLabel: themeLabel }); } } } return results; } function _search(query) { if (!query || query.length < 2) return []; const q = query.toLowerCase(); const all = _getAllDocs(); const matched = []; for (const d of all) { if (d.code.toLowerCase().includes(q) || d.titre.toLowerCase().includes(q)) { matched.push(d); if (matched.length >= 10) break; } } return matched; } function _escHtml(s) { return s.replace(/&/g,'&').replace(//g,'>').replace(/"/g,'"'); } function _renderResults(container, results) { // Note: code/titre/themeLabel come from static THEMES data (developer-controlled, not user input) // The search query itself is never injected into the HTML if (!results.length) { container.textContent = ''; const noRes = document.createElement('div'); noRes.className = 'search-no-result'; noRes.textContent = 'Aucun document trouve.'; container.appendChild(noRes); } else { container.textContent = ''; results.forEach(function(r) { const item = document.createElement('div'); item.className = 'search-result-item'; item.dataset.theme = r.themeId; const left = document.createElement('div'); if (r.code) { const codeSpan = document.createElement('span'); codeSpan.className = 'search-result-code'; codeSpan.textContent = r.code; left.appendChild(codeSpan); } left.appendChild(document.createTextNode(r.titre)); const right = document.createElement('span'); right.className = 'search-result-theme'; right.textContent = r.themeLabel; item.appendChild(left); item.appendChild(right); item.addEventListener('click', function() { APP.switchTab(r.themeId); container.style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('global-search').value = ''; }); container.appendChild(item); }); } } function init() { const input = document.getElementById('global-search'); const container = document.getElementById('search-results'); if (!input || !container) return; input.addEventListener('input', function() { const q = input.value.trim(); if (q.length < 2) { container.style.display = 'none'; return; } const results = _search(q); _renderResults(container, results); container.style.display = 'block'; }); document.addEventListener('click', function(e) { if (!input.contains(e.target) && !container.contains(e.target)) { container.style.display = 'none'; } }); } return { init: init }; })(); // ── Init ────────────────────────────────────────────── async function init() { await AUTH.initDefaultCreds(); AUTH.loadCreds(); // Auto-login si appareil enregistré const deviceUser = localStorage.getItem('smq_device_user'); const deviceTs = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('smq_device_ts') || '0'); if (deviceUser && (Date.now() - deviceTs < 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)) { const allUsers = ADMIN.getAllUsers(); if (allUsers[deviceUser]) { AUTH.saveSession(deviceUser); LOGIN.init(); APP.show(AUTH.getSession()); return; } } LOGIN.init(); SEARCH.init(); const sess = AUTH.getSession(); if (sess) APP.show(sess); } document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
